This file contains solutions for each single day (just one per day, more likely exist).

The format is: day/month [weekday]

So if you're looking for Thursday 8th of April (as shown in the example imagine on the website), scroll down to:

7 6 3 3 5 5 9 
7 6 6 6 6 8 9 
7 7 7 8 8 8 9 
X X X X X 8 9 

All puzzle pieces are numbered 0 to 9. And the edge of the puzzle is marked with an 'X'.
